<script src='/s/waset/ext/jquery.jscroll.min.js'></script>
<script>
var searchCities=[]
$('.cityCountry').each(function(){
    searchCities[searchCities.length]=this.innerHTML})
searchCities = searchCities.sort().filter(function(el,i,a){return i==a.indexOf(el);})
var months = ["Jan", "Feb", "Mar", "Apr", "May", "Jun", "Jul", "Aug", "Sep", "Oct", "Nov", "Dec"]
var dbSearchDates=[]
$('.dates').each(function(){
    dbSearchDates[dbSearchDates.length]=this.innerHTML.substring(0, 3)})
var dbSearchCity = []
$(searchCities).each(function(){
	quote = '"'+this+'"'
    dbSearchCity[dbSearchCity.length]= "<a href='#' onClick='searchCity(this);return false;'>"+this+"</a>"
  })
$('.searchInPage #searchCity').html(dbSearchCity.join(''))
var strSearchDate = []
$(months).each(function(){
    for(i in dbSearchDates)
        if(dbSearchDates[i]==this){
			quote = '"'+this+'"'
            strSearchDate[strSearchDate.length] = "<a href='#' onClick='searchDate(this);return false;'>"+this+"</a>"
            return;
            }
  })
$('.cityBox').unbind('click').click(function(){
	var clasMiyim = $(this).hasClass('bigger')
    $('.bigger').removeClass('bigger')
	if(clasMiyim)
		return;
    var cities = $('.cityBox');
    var eureka =9999;
    for(c in cities)
        if(cities[c]==this){
            eureka = c;
            l = cities.length;
            $(cities[c]).addClass('bigger');
            switch(c%3 ){
                case 0: break;
                case 1:
                    $(cities[c-1]).after(cities[c]);
                    break;
                case 2:
                    $(cities[c-2]).after(cities[c]);
                    break;
                
            }
            break;
        }
})
$('.searchInPage #searchDate').html(strSearchDate.join(''))
function searchCity(that){
	if($(that).hasClass('selected')){
		$('#searchCityOpener').html('by City');
		return $(that).removeClass('selected') && searchInPage();
		}
	$('#searchDateOpener').html('by Date');
	$('#searchCity a').removeClass('selected');
	$('#searchDate a').removeClass('selected');
	$(that).addClass('selected');
	$('#searchCityOpener').html(that.innerHTML);
	searchInPage();
}
function searchDate (that){
	if($(that).hasClass('selected')){
		$('#searchDateOpener').html('by Date');
		return $(that).removeClass('selected') && searchInPage();
		}
	$('#searchCityOpener').html('by City');
	$('#searchDate a').removeClass('selected');
	$('#searchCity a').removeClass('selected');

	$(that).addClass('selected');
	$('#searchDateOpener').html(that.innerHTML);
	searchInPage();
}
$('#searchYear a').click(function(){searchYear(this.id);})
$('#year2014Selector').click(function(){ $('#yearSelector').html(2014);searchYear()})
$('#year2015Selector').click(function(){ $('#yearSelector').html(2015);searchYear()})
function searchYear(yearId){
	var year = $('#yearSelector').html();
	if(yearId == 'yearSmall'){
		if(year>2012) 
			year--;
	}else if(yearId =='yearBigger'){
		if(year<2015) 
			year++;
	}
	document.getElementById('yearSelector').innerHTML = year;
	searchInPage();
}
function searchInPage(){
    timer = 500;
	var date = $('#searchDate .selected').html();
	var city = $('#searchCity .selected').html();
	var year = $('#yearSelector').html();
	var selectedNumber = 0;
	$('.cityBox').hide(timer-200);
	$('.cityBox'+'.year'+year).each(function(index){
		timer = (Math.random()*300)+200;
		if(city){
			if($('.cityCountry', this).html()==city){
				if(date){
					dateCur = $('.dates', this).html().substring(0,3);
					if(dateCur == date){
						$(this).show(timer);
						selectedNumber++;
					}
				} else{
					$(this).show(timer);
					selectedNumber++;

				}
			}
		}else if(date){
			dateCur = $('.dates', this).html().substring(0,3);
			if(dateCur == date){
				$(this).show(timer);
				selectedNumber++;
			}
		}else{
			$(this).show(timer);
			selectedNumber++;

		}
		
	})
	if(!selectedNumber){
	$('.cityBox').each(function(index){
		if(city){
			if($('.cityCountry', this).html()==city){
				if(date){
					dateCur = $('.dates', this).html().substring(0,3);
					if(dateCur == date){
						$(this).show(timer);
						selectedNumber++;
					}
				} else{
					$(this).show(timer);
					selectedNumber++;

				}
			}
		}else if(date){
			dateCur = $('.dates', this).html().substring(0,3);
			if(dateCur == date){
				$(this).show(timer);
				selectedNumber++;
			}
		}else{
			$(this).show(timer);
			selectedNumber++;

		}
		
	})
	}
	return false;
}

function searchInPageOpening (){
    timer = 500;
	var selectedNumber = 0;
	$('.cityBox'+'.year2014').each(function(index){
		timer = (Math.random()*300)+200;
		dateCur = ($('.dates', this).html().substring(0,3));
		if(["", "Jan", "Feb", "Mar", "Apr", "May", "Jun", "Jul"].indexOf(dateCur)>0)
			$(this).show(timer);
	})
	return false;
}
$('.scroll').jscroll({
    loadingHtml: '<img src="/i/a/loadingPacman.gif" alt="Loading" /> Loading...',
    padding: 20,
    nextSelector: '#loadMoreConferences'
});
searchInPageOpening();
</script>
